A monetary union was established in 1999 and came into full force in 2002, and is composed of 19 EU member states which use the euro currency.'], ['Mohamed Mimoune', 'How Moha defended his European Union title?\nOn 31 March 2017, Mohamed defeated Jussi Koivula by unanimous decision to retain the European Union title.'], ['Jussi Koivula', 'How Moha defended his European Union title?\nOn 31 March 2017, Mohamed defeated Jussi Koivula by unanimous decision to retain the European Union title.']]]
